<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">1986–87 UEFA Cup</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
</div>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><script>function mfTempOpenSection(id){var block=document.getElementById("mf-section-"+id);block.className+=" open-block";block.previousSibling.className+=" open-block";}</script><table class="infobox vcalendar" style="width:22em">
<caption class="summary">1986–87 UEFA Cup</caption>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Dates</th>
<td>16 September 1986 – 20 May 1987</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align:center">Final positions</th>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Champions</th>
<td><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden"><img alt="Sweden" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1600" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/23px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/35px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/46px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/IFK_G%C3%B6teborg" title="IFK Göteborg">IFK Göteborg</a> <span class="nowrap">(2nd title)</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Runners-up</th>
<td><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland"><img alt="Scotland" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1000" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Flag_of_Scotland.svg/23px-Flag_of_Scotland.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Flag_of_Scotland.svg/35px-Flag_of_Scotland.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Flag_of_Scotland.svg/46px-Flag_of_Scotland.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Dundee_United_F.C." title="Dundee United F.C.">Dundee United</a></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="noprint" colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<div style="float: left;">← <a href="/wiki/1985%E2%80%9386_UEFA_Cup" title="1985–86 UEFA Cup">1985–86</a></div>
<div style="float: right;"><a href="/wiki/1987%E2%80%9388_UEFA_Cup" title="1987–88 UEFA Cup">1987–88</a> →</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>The <b>1986–87 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UEFA_Cup" title="UEFA Cup">UEFA Cup</a></b> was won by <a href="/wiki/IFK_G%C3%B6teborg" title="IFK Göteborg">IFK Göteborg</a> of Sweden on aggregate over <a href="/wiki/Dundee_United_F.C." title="Dundee United F.C.">Dundee United</a> of Scotland. This was the second season in which all English clubs were banned from European football competitions, preventing <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham United</a>, <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sheffield_Wednesday_F.C." title="Sheffield Wednesday F.C.">Sheffield Wednesday</a> and <a href="/wiki/Oxford_United_F.C." title="Oxford United F.C.">Oxford United</a> from competing in the 1986–87 UEFA Cup.</p>
<p></p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_leg">Second leg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1986%E2%80%9387_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Second leg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="First_leg_2">First leg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1986%E2%80%9387_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: First leg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="vevent" style="width: 100%; background-color: transparent; clear:both">

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_leg_3">Second leg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1986%E2%80%9387_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Second leg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
